  * [ ingridcold](ingridcold)

  * | Joined Feb 2016  | Status: Trader | [6 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=448185)

I have been testing the Sunday gap for some time on a few pairs and I was wondering if ts it possible to create EA with the following inputs (that can be changed to fit the different pairs). I checked some already existing EAs but they do not allow to modify all the inputs and also none of them takes the spread into account  
  
Trade to fill the gap  
\- open trade only if gap is bigger than X pips  
\- open trade only if spread is smaller than X pips  
\- risk per trade 2% of account  
  
Stop loss. Two cases  
\- if gap is between X and Y pips, then SL is set to SL=Gap size +the current spread (spread should always be taken into account when placing the SL)  
-if gap is more than X pips then set SL to SL =10pips + the current spread  
  
Would be nice if its possible to have the SL flexible to fit different rules. For example, if the gap is between 5 and 10 pips..SL is gap size + spread. IF gap is 11-20pips....Sl is fixed at 10 pips...if between 21 and 50 SL is fixed at 20..and so on

Good day GAP traders,  
  
I have read all the postings in this thread and find it interesting. In my experience I do better with the DAILY TF. I look for the indicator to ARROW signal a direction but not enter immediately. To me I am willing to let the first day go by and if the indicator was CORRECT in its prediction then I am willing to take on DAY #2 in the direction indicated by the arrows. I also basket trade with this concept and have done well. I use SL but DO NOT use TP but followup with a manual SL or if going to bed, a TS instead. One more thing, paying attention to PIN BARS IN THE DAILY TF can really pay off. Here is my latest win in that regard. I also favor PENDING ORDERS and try to let the price action sweep me in, less stress in my opinion.

GAP BAR ALERT ON EU/NZ.  
I place a SELL STOP UNDERNEATH THE TAIL OF THE ARROW w/STOP LOSS ABOVE ABOUT 500 PIPS. I use the CROSSHAIR TOOL at the top of the chart, click on it, place on chart, click and drag from a GRID LINE TO THE NEXT GRID LINE, look at Middle number and it should give you an idea of how much is needed for the price to breath. POINTS TO CONSIDER:  
1\. PRICE BAR IS DOWN  
2\. DOUBLE LINE IS BEING CRUSHED  
3\. GAP ARROW APPEARED ON A NON-OPENING DAY, looks to me like someone is anxious to get in position before major move. If not, it should not trigger and you can delete it later.  
4\. THERE IS ALSO A GREAT PIN BAR SHOWING.

  * [#414](/thread/post/8925998#post8925998 "Post Permalink")

  * May 14, 2016 2:29pm  May 14, 2016 2:29pm 

  * [ Moonbeam15](moonbeam15)

  * | Joined Oct 2015  | Status: Trader | [222 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=429198)

Hello ahamidz,  
  
Yes the arrow is the GAP ARROW INDICATOR, WITH ONE CHANGE UNDER INPUTS, THE SIZE GAP I USE IS (100) NOT (5).  
What I am trying to show you is the ARROW CAN BE POSSIBLY TRADED TWO WAYS.  
First: The GAP ARROW IS MADE ON THE SUNDAY/MONDAY BAR. I PREFER JUST TO WAIT UNTIL 2:00 PST DAY CHANGE, WHICH WOULD BE TUESDAY TO PLACE ANY PENDING POSITION ORDER.  
Second: I LOOK FOR ANY BAR THAT HAS A HIGH CHANCE OF TAKING OFF, FOR INSTANCE, "STAR BAR", "PIN BAR". A STAR BAR CAN HAVE PENDING ORDER AT THE TOP (TO BUY) AND THE BOTTOM (TO SELL) AT THE SAME TIME. WHEN ONE TRIGGERS THE OTHER IS CANCELLED.  
THE PEN BAR HAS A MASSIVE TAIL SHOWING TOTAL REJECTION TO THE "BEARS", IT IS AS THOUGH EVERYONE IS ON BOARD FOR, IN THIS CASE, A UPWARD MOVE, WHICH I ENJOYED VERY MUCH. DO NOT FORGET THAT EACH PENDING ORDER HAS A LEAST A 500 STOP LOSS WITH IT. NO UNCOVERED POSITIONS PLEASE.  
Third: WHEN THE ARROW APPEARS AND SUNDAY/MONDAY BAR IS DONE, I PLACE A PENDING ORDER ON THE TAIL END OF THE ARROW JUST IN CASE THERE IS A SLIGHT CHANCE OF A QUICK BUCK TO BE MADE. IN THE CASE OF THE "PIN BAR" IT WAS VERY GOOD TO DO SO WHEN IT SWUNG MUCH LOWER FIRST BEFORE RECOVERING ALL THE WAY BACK UP AND CHANGING THE COLOR OF THE BAR. IN THE LOWER TIME FRAMES YOU SEE THIS ALL THE TIME AND WITH THE SPREAD AND PRICE ACTION YOU STAND A CHANCE OF SUCCEEDING, BUT A "DAILY PIN BAR" LOOOOK OUT, THIS COULD BE A BIG MOVE, AND I STATED THAT IN MY POSTED CHART BEFORE THE MOVE.  
  
LETS START WITH THIS AND WAIT FOR NEXT WEEK AND SEE WHAT WE GET TO DO!! 

Attached Image (click to enlarge)

If you like gap trading... You may also Like Liquidty gap trading... Whats a liquidty gap?   
A liquidty gap is basicly a spike... A gap where market had no liquidty and spiked right though it..   
Spikes are very simalar to gaps 

The only system that will work is one designed by and for yourself.

  * [#449](/thread/post/8936304#post8936304 "Post Permalink")

  * May 20, 2016 6:28am  May 20, 2016 6:28am 

  * [ Moonbeam15](moonbeam15)

  * | Joined Oct 2015  | Status: Trader | [222 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=429198)

TIME: 2:08 PST. NEW AND LAST BAR OF THE WEEK.  
Well here we are at the last bar of the week forming. This bar will help the BIG BOYS line up for next week. We should look for certain type bars I have mentioned in past posts, it is only two of them so no groaning. For one reason, "they work pretty well".  
I do not use the "CANDLE STICK TYPE BAR", I use the regular bar that shows the same information. I like to physically see the GAP better. In the chart shown is a "LARGE DOJI", a trader could place a BUY STOP ON THE HIGH END AND A SELL STOP ON THE LOW END WITH APPROPRIATE STOP LOSS ON BOTH ORDERS IN THE PENDING MODE. When one side fills, cancel the other.  
JUST A THOUGHT. The DOJI BAR is like a big question mark from all traders, bull or bear, trying to see which way it will go next.

  * [#454](/thread/post/8938387#post8938387 "Post Permalink")

  * May 21, 2016 1:04pm  May 21, 2016 1:04pm 

  * [ Moonbeam15](moonbeam15)

  * | Joined Oct 2015  | Status: Trader | [222 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=429198)

Thank you ismael360. Not perfect but profitable. Like everyone else I have to fight with my GREED MONSTER. Something I forgot to mention about the "GAP ARROW SIZE" in color area, I use the #3 ARROW SIZE. I do this because I use the tail end of the ARROW as my "STOP LOSS PLACEMENT TO START WITH" then manually trail it with the price movement, its sort of a game of "KEEP AWAY" and I hope not to stop out to soon. What really concerns me is sometimes even waiting for the NEW BAR CHANGE TO START TUESDAY BAR, has in the past in some of the charts gone horribly wrong and continued against the arrow direction. So I plan to use two positions, one up and one down to surround the price in case it wants to break out. When one side fills I will probably drop the other.

Here is a continuation of the chart above. Once the "BUZZER" started to form the flat line the price action has stalled. I believe it is the three day holiday coming this week-end that has affected the action. Just my opinion. I did take a little profit on the last up swing. Glad I got out. Another interesting point is a new out of no where "GAP ARROW" showed up on the THURSDAY BAR.
